The beauty of Zhenjiang is beyond stunning, and this stay at Crowne Plaza Zhenjiang Zhaohe should have added a perfect impression to this trip. The location and the high-speed rail station are only about 10 minutes' drive away. Check-in was smooth. After learning that I was a member, I was given a member drink coupon. The lobby is clean and tidy, the girl at the front desk is enthusiastic, and the river view room faces the river. Although the weather is a bit hazy, on a clear day you can still clearly see the lake island and riverside scenery opposite. The hotel is very close to Beigu Mountain and can be reached on foot. It is a bit far to walk to Xijin Ferry and Jinshan Temple, but the bus is only 2 stops (3 stops) and 5 stops respectively, which is very convenient (Zhenjiang bus is 1 yuan). Taking a taxi to Xijindu costs about 8 yuan, and taking a taxi to Jiaoshan costs about 12 yuan. I am very grateful to the hotel‚Äôs customer service manager, Manager Tang Gan. When we asked about the problem, he was very enthusiastic. Not only did he help solve the problem quickly, but he also gave us a small gift box of Zhenjiang balsamic vinegar and fruits, which made us feel at home. After all, it is from Crown. Service, Crown quality. The breakfast in the hotel is very rich, and the executive lounge on the 23rd floor has a good view. It is quiet and suitable for slowly enjoying the river view. The overall experience is very good. I will choose to stay at Crowne Plaza Zhaohe next time if I have the opportunity.
